				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Uns ist ein Kind geboren (Kuhnau, Johann)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div id="contentSub">(Redirected from <a href="/index.php?title=Uns_ist_ein_Kind_geboren,_BWV_142_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)&amp;redirect=no" title="Uns ist ein Kind geboren, BWV 142 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Uns ist ein Kind geboren, BWV 142 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)</a>)</div><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div><table style="padding:0.25em; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto; background-color:rgb(238,232,170); width:65%; border:1px solid #a3bfb1"><tr><td align="center"><b>Authorship Note</b><br />Formerly attributed to Johann Sebastian Bach as his BWV 142.</td></tr></table></div>
<p><br />
</p>
<div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>8 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1720?
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>Cantata for Christmas Day, formerly attributed to <a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Johann Sebastian Bach</a>, but probably composed by Johann Kuhnau.
</p><p>Publication in 1884 seems to have been of some arrangements (by Graf von Waldersee) only according to HMB?, full publication may have awaited 1894? - Schissel
</p>
